- `Completed foundation`: loyalty business detail now also reuses the shared member cross-surface rail, so protected loyalty detail follow-up stays aligned with the rest of the member portal instead of a route-local CTA block
- `Completed foundation`: loyalty overview now also consumes `my/businesses`, so joined business cards render with image/category/city context instead of only flat account summaries
- `Completed foundation`: business-scoped promotions feed and promotion-interaction tracking now run through the canonical member contracts on `/loyalty/[businessId]`
- `Completed foundation`: `/loyalty` now also consumes public business discovery plus public category-kinds metadata so loyalty-ready businesses remain browseable even before the member joins
- `Completed foundation`: public loyalty overview now also consumes live public CMS pages plus public categories for a storefront-continuation window, so signed-out loyalty discovery stays connected to published content and catalog browse follow-up without needing new backend contracts
- `Completed foundation`: `/loyalty/[businessId]` now falls back to canonical public business detail for anonymous or not-yet-joined members and exposes a direct join action through the canonical member join contract when the member session is healthy
- `Completed foundation`: public loyalty business detail now also consumes live public CMS pages plus public categories for a storefront-continuation window, so pre-join loyalty routes stay connected to public content and catalog browse follow-up without needing new backend contracts
- `Completed foundation`: `/loyalty` now also supports query-driven proximity discovery and a server-rendered coordinate preview using the same public loyalty-filtered discovery result set
- `Completed foundation`: `/loyalty/[businessId]` now also prepares canonical browser-side scan sessions for accrual or redemption, including branch selection and reward selection, while keeping the short-lived scan token in a web-owned cookie instead of the URL
- `Completed foundation`: `/loyalty/[businessId]` now also renders a real QR image from the canonical short-lived scan token for contract visibility on the web route
- `Completed foundation`: loyalty business detail now also follows the shared member-portal navigation model, and scan-session cookie/action handling now clears stale or mismatched prepared-token state instead of letting browser-local scan state drift silently
- `Depends on auth/account`: join flows and any scan-preparation UX still depend on the same member session foundation and should stay aligned with mobile-facing contracts
- `Decision made`: `Darwin.Web` should not assume browser camera/scanner or barcode-handling ownership for loyalty. The current scan-preparation/QR slice is only provisional contract consumption, and later web loyalty behavior should be designed around explicit web requirements such as direct point accrual/redemption for store-enabled businesses rather than mobile-like scanner workflows
- `Completed`: loyalty overview and loyalty business detail in `Darwin.Web` now also surface storefront-continuation windows fed by live public CMS pages plus public categories, so protected loyalty routes stay connected to public content and catalog follow-up without requiring new backend contracts
- `Decision made`: public loyalty discovery is storefront-safe and should stay visible even when a member is signed out or has not joined a business yet; member-only balances, promotions, and timelines stay behind the authenticated portal
- `Depends on WebApi/backend`: full viewport map consumption through `public/businesses/map` still needs either a loyalty-active filter or another storefront-safe contract shape before `Darwin.Web` can rely on that endpoint without mixing non-loyalty businesses into the loyalty discovery surface
- `Later-phase only`: explicit web-specific loyalty accrual/redemption flows for store-enabled businesses, interactive map-pan/zoom flows if still needed, push-heavy engagement surfaces, and deeper loyalty gamification outside the current contract set

#### Orders / invoices / payments

- `Unblocked now`: public cart, shipping-rate estimation, checkout intent, order placement, payment-intent handoff, payment completion, and order confirmation already exist in `Darwin.WebApi`
- `Unblocked now`: member order history, order detail, invoice history, invoice detail, retry-payment, and plain-text document endpoints already exist in `Darwin.WebApi`
- `Unblocked now`: Stripe-first and DHL-first operator support now exists in WebAdmin across payments, refunds, webhooks, shipments, and carrier/support triage, so web checkout/payment flows now have real operational backing
- `Completed foundation`: `Darwin.Web` now has a public cart slice with stable anonymous storefront identity, add-to-cart from product detail, cart item quantity/remove actions, and visible degraded-mode handling around public cart API failures
- `Completed foundation`: `Darwin.Web` now also has a public checkout slice with server-rendered address capture, live checkout-intent preview, shipping-method selection, order placement, and storefront confirmation/payment-handoff entry points
- `Completed foundation`: public cart now also consumes coupon apply/clear and shows richer line-level net/VAT/add-on context from the canonical cart snapshot
- `Completed foundation`: public cart now also shows storefront follow-up products from the canonical public catalog contract plus explicit next-step guidance, so continue-shopping and conversion follow-up do not depend only on one summary card
- `Completed foundation`: public cart now also reuses saved member addresses when a browser member session exists, so checkout readiness can surface before the shopper leaves the cart route for checkout
- `Completed foundation`: public cart now also surfaces member profile/preferences/address readiness together, so signed-in shoppers can verify identity, phone/channel readiness, and address coverage before moving into checkout
- `Completed foundation`: checkout summary now also surfaces coupon state plus shipment-mass/shipping-country context from the live intent instead of keeping shipping/tax presentation minimal
- `Completed foundation`: checkout now also shows readiness signals plus a live order-review panel for current cart lines, so order placement is no longer gated only by the address form and total summary
- `Completed foundation`: checkout now also reuses saved member addresses when a browser member session is available, while preserving manual entry and degraded-mode visibility when the member address-book contract is unavailable
- `Completed foundation`: checkout now also reuses canonical member profile identity for name/phone prefill when a member session exists but no saved address is selected, so the route can still start from member context before the address book is populated
- `Completed foundation`: checkout now also surfaces recent member invoice attention inside the route, so signed-in shoppers can keep open billing follow-up visible before placing a new order
- `Completed foundation`: checkout now also surfaces a dedicated payment-continuity window before order placement, so projected payable total, billing attention, and account handoff stay explicit instead of hiding behind the final submit action
- `Completed foundation`: the cart route now also surfaces explicit opportunity and readiness panels, so shoppers can see the strongest adjacent offer plus basket readiness before leaving the route for checkout
- `Completed foundation`: checkout now also surfaces explicit confidence and attention panels, so order-readiness, billing follow-up, phone verification, and address-book coverage stay visible at the final conversion step
- `Completed foundation`: order detail and invoice detail now also reuse the shared member cross-surface rail, so protected commerce detail follow-up stays aligned with the overview routes instead of route-specific CTA groups
- `Completed foundation`: auth-required member entry points plus unavailable order/invoice/loyalty detail states now also reuse the shared member cross-surface rail, so protected degraded-state follow-up stays on the same continuity model as healthy portal routes
- `Completed foundation`: storefront confirmation now also reconciles hosted-checkout return/cancel flows through the canonical payment-completion endpoint, using a web-owned handoff cookie only as transport glue instead of treating return URLs as the source of truth
- `Completed foundation`: storefront confirmation now also keeps post-checkout guidance visible, including payment-attention vs paid next-step messaging, explicit account/order-history follow-up, and a stable order-reference panel instead of behaving like a passive receipt-only route
- `Completed foundation`: auth-required and post-checkout follow-up links now also sanitize app-local return targets centrally, and confirmation status messaging now derives from the authoritative confirmation snapshot instead of trusting query-carried order/payment status text
- `Completed foundation`: auth-required member entry points now also render route-summary plus cross-surface follow-up panels, so protected routes stay consistent with the wider portal orientation model instead of degrading to a minimal access wall
- `Completed foundation`: cart, checkout, and confirmation now also share breadcrumb-style route orientation plus explicit cross-surface handoff cards, so the conversion chain stays connected to the wider storefront system instead of behaving like detached transactional pages
- `Completed foundation`: cart, checkout, confirmation, and their empty/unavailable follow-up states now also reuse a shared commerce continuation rail, so public conversion continuity stays on one shared component instead of route-local CTA clusters
- `Completed foundation`: cart and checkout now also surface a shared anonymous account-handoff panel carrying a sanitized `returnPath` into sign-in/register/activation/password help, so commerce routes keep account recovery one step away without dropping the current conversion intent
- `Completed foundation`: public commerce hardening now also normalizes quantity, coupon, country-code, and allowed status-query inputs so cart/checkout/confirmation redirects and form posts stay explicit instead of trusting raw browser values
- `Completed foundation`: authenticated member order history/detail and invoice history/detail now render through the browser-session layer and can trigger member-scoped payment retry handoff
- `Completed foundation`: order-history storefront merchandising now also ranks visible product follow-up by strongest savings signal, so post-purchase history can surface clearer next-buy opportunities instead of a raw public-product list
- `Completed foundation`: invoice-history storefront merchandising now also ranks visible product follow-up by strongest savings signal, so billing history can surface clearer next-buy opportunities instead of a raw public-product list
  - `Completed foundation`: orders, invoices, and loyalty surfaces now also share the same member-portal navigation model as profile/preferences/addresses, so post-purchase and loyalty follow-up no longer feel like detached routes
- `Completed foundation`: member order detail now also renders shipment/payment snapshots, linked invoice follow-up, and direct document download from the canonical member order contract
- `Completed foundation`: member invoice detail now also renders canonical payment summary and direct document download from the member invoice contract
- `Completed foundation`: protected order/invoice detail storefront merchandising now also ranks visible product follow-up by strongest savings signal, so commerce detail routes can surface clearer next-buy opportunities instead of a raw public-product list
  - `Completed foundation`: member order/invoice history routes now also expose explicit history-window summaries, and their empty states retain account/catalog follow-up actions instead of collapsing into passive archive placeholders
- `Decision made`: anonymous storefront cart identity is currently owned by `Darwin.Web` through a stable web cookie until a broader browser-session/BFF transport is introduced
- `Decision made`: the current public cart contract does not expose product title/media snapshots for line display, so `Darwin.Web` may keep a lightweight local display snapshot for UX continuity without changing the API source of truth for cart totals and row identity
- `Decision made`: successful public order placement must clear the web-owned anonymous cart cookie and local display snapshot so the storefront does not fall back into stale cart `not-found` states after checkout
- `Depends on billing/compliance`: checkout, invoice, and payment UX must stay aware of B2B/B2C tax profile, VAT completeness, invoice readiness, and archive/e-invoice baseline signals without pretending the deeper compliance engine is already complete
- `Depends on WebApi/backend`: richer public cart display contracts, anonymous-to-member cart merge behavior, payment-state polling/completion visibility, and deeper checkout composition still need front-office integration work and may require additive API composition in practice
- `Later-phase only`: full provider callbacks/verification hardening, alternative PSPs, richer refund/return/RMA self-service, and dispute-heavy finance UX

#### Localization / config-driven behavior

- `Unblocked now`: the platform now has explicit localization ownership guidance, locale/fallback visibility in admin/CRM, and member profile locale/time-zone/currency fields that web flows can respect from day one
- `Unblocked now`: site settings and business setup already expose ownership splits around localization, communication, branding, payment, shipping, and tax defaults, so config-driven web planning can align to real platform governance
- `Completed foundation`: `Darwin.Web` now treats `de-DE` and `en-US` as the active front-office cultures, persists culture through cookie/query-string switching, and keeps shell fallback copy aligned with the current culture
- `Completed foundation`: `Darwin.Web` now has a resource-bundle localization foundation under `src/Darwin.Web/src/localization/resources`, and shared shell/catalog/storefront-commerce plus account-edit/member-commerce and loyalty discovery/public-detail copy now run on that path so future languages can be added without reworking component structure
- `Completed foundation`: `Darwin.Web` now validates member order/invoice document URLs before rendering download anchors, so malformed WebApi document paths degrade into observable unavailable states instead of broken or over-permissive links
- `Completed foundation`: `Darwin.Web` now routes loyalty discovery map links and linked-invoice handoffs through locale-aware paths, so those surfaces no longer drop users out of the active localized route tree
- `Completed foundation`: `Darwin.Web` now validates optional public loyalty-business website URLs before rendering external anchors, so malformed public metadata degrades into absence instead of unsafe or broken external links
- `Completed foundation`: `Darwin.Web` now resolves loyalty public/discovery/member-overview media URLs through the backend-safe helper, so malformed business image paths degrade into placeholders instead of raw `img` sources
- `Completed foundation`: `Darwin.Web` now resolves catalog, cart, checkout, and product-detail media URLs through the backend-safe helper as well, so public commerce image rendering degrades into placeholders instead of trusting raw payload URLs
- `Completed foundation`: safe public website links and member document downloads that open in new tabs now flow through a shared hardened external-link contract with `noopener noreferrer` plus no-referrer isolation, so external/document handoff follows the same tab-isolation baseline instead of drifting route by route
- `Completed foundation`: `Darwin.Web` now sanitizes CMS page HTML and product full-description HTML before injection, removing obvious high-risk tags and inline script hooks instead of trusting raw backend HTML wholesale
- `Completed foundation`: that lightweight fragment sanitizer now also strips unquoted inline event handlers and unquoted `javascript:` `href/src` attributes, and now also rejects dangerous `formaction` / `xlink:href` / `srcdoc` patterns, so malformed dangerous fragments do not bypass the earlier quoted-attribute checks
- `Completed foundation`: CMS detail now also sanitizes its non-summary HTML fallback before injection, so heading-less pages do not bypass that same fragment-hardening path
- `Completed foundation`: `Darwin.Web` now sanitizes cart snapshot product links at both cookie-read and render time, so browser-local cart state cannot redirect storefront return links outside the intended app-local route tree
- `Completed foundation`: the default storefront typography stack now also uses local/system body and display fonts instead of naming external-first faces like `Manrope` and `Fraunces`, so the web baseline stays deterministic in restricted/offline environments without depending on non-local font availability
- `Completed foundation`: profile editing, preferences, address-book management, loyalty overview/discovery, loyalty map preview, public pre-join loyalty detail, and signed-in loyalty business detail now consume the member resource bundles instead of app-local text blocks
- `Completed foundation`: route-level metadata for shell, Home, CMS index/detail fallbacks, catalog, checkout, account, orders, invoices, and loyalty now resolves through the same culture-aware resource path instead of static page titles/descriptions
- `Completed foundation`: loyalty overview and loyalty business-detail routes now also load their noindex metadata through the shared observed SEO loader instead of route-local `buildNoIndexMetadata(...)`, so the member-loyalty lane no longer keeps its own SEO assembly branch outside the broader route-metadata pipeline
- `Completed foundation`: the `mock-checkout` route now resolves its metadata, page title/description, and failure-reason handoff through the commerce resource bundle instead of keeping a route-local `culture === "de-DE"` branch and English fallback literals
- `Completed foundation`: the `MockCheckoutPage` action cards now also consume the commerce-bundle unavailable label instead of keeping a component-local `URL unavailable` literal, so that local hosted-checkout surface no longer splits between resource-backed route copy and a dangling English fallback inside the page body
- `Completed foundation`: local web-owned validation and flash messages for register/activation/password/sign-in, cart/checkout, payment retry, profile/preferences/addresses, and loyalty join/scan/promotion flows now travel as localization keys and resolve inside the UI resource bundles instead of baking English-only fallback text into server actions
- `Completed foundation`: generic public/member API fallback messages and CMS degraded-mode UI copy now also resolve through resource bundles, so network/not-found/http fallback states no longer depend on English-only client literals
- `Completed foundation`: generic public/member/auth/payment-handoff API wrappers in `Darwin.Web` now only surface backend problem messages when they arrive as `i18n:` localization tokens; otherwise they fall back to the route-localized bundle message instead of leaking raw plain-English problem details into the storefront UI
- `Completed foundation`: CMS detail unavailable state plus catalog index/detail now also expose route-summary diagnostics and actionable no-result/unavailable follow-up CTAs, so degraded public storefront routes stay observable and navigable instead of collapsing into passive warning blocks
- `Completed foundation`: cart, checkout, and confirmation now also expose route-summary diagnostics plus stronger empty/unavailable follow-up CTAs, so the conversion path stays observable and actionable instead of degrading into passive panels
- `Completed foundation`: locale-aware money/date formatting in `Darwin.Web` now resolves through the supported-cultures runtime contract with language-variant fallback and default-culture fallback instead of assuming a hardcoded `de-DE` baseline inside shared helpers
- `Completed foundation`: private and mixed account/commerce/member routes now explicitly emit `noindex` metadata while public Home/CMS/catalog routes stay indexable through the centralized SEO helper, so storefront SEO policy is no longer implicit or route-by-route drift-prone
- `Completed foundation`: public Home/CMS/catalog routes now expose stable locale-prefixed canonical URLs, and index-level public routes emit language alternates where slug mapping is not ambiguous
- `Completed foundation`: loyalty overview/discovery plus public and signed-in loyalty business surfaces now resolve status-bearing warnings and storefront route summaries through member-bundle status labels instead of rendering raw `ok` / `not-found` / `network-error` style tokens in the UI
- `Completed foundation`: CMS and product detail routes now also emit localized `hreflang` alternates by matching canonical public ids across the current `de-DE` / `en-US` public sets, so detail-page language alternates no longer depend on slug-parity guesses for the current storefront baseline
- `Completed foundation`: public sitemap inventory now also emits localized CMS and product detail entries by matching canonical public ids across the current `de-DE` / `en-US` public sets, so multilingual public discovery is no longer limited to index-level routes
- `Completed foundation`: localized CMS and product detail inventory now also loads through shared cached storefront discovery helpers, so metadata alternates plus sitemap discovery reuse one canonical multilingual inventory path instead of refetching public sets independently
- `Completed foundation`: CMS and catalog browse cores now also load through the same shared observed-loader pattern as route, commerce, and multilingual inventory contexts, so public discovery assembly is more consistent, cache-aware, and traceable across list/detail/SEO surfaces
- `Completed foundation`: storefront continuation snapshots for live CMS/category/product follow-up now also load through that same shared observed-loader pattern with explicit health summaries, so continuation windows no longer stay as the last route-local discovery assembly branch
- `Completed foundation`: shell menu loading and cart view-model assembly now also run through the same shared observed-loader and health-summary path, so shell chrome and cart entry no longer keep manual diagnostics/caching branches outside the broader storefront infrastructure
- `Decision made`: profile locale editing now follows the supported-cultures config instead of accepting an unrestricted locale string inside the first self-service slice
- `Decision made`: until the web introduces crawlable path- or host-based locale URLs, sitemap/canonical discovery should stay on the default-culture public paths and not pretend that cookie/query-based culture switching creates stable alternate-language URLs
- `Decision made`: additive languages beyond the current `de-DE` / `en-US` public baseline may still need a stronger localized-slug linking contract if canonical id matching is no longer sufficient or public-set fan-out becomes too expensive
- `Depends on localization`: the platform does not yet have complete multilingual CMS/template management, so web must be built localization-ready without assuming full translated content operations already exist
- `Depends on compliance/billing`: tax, invoice, and payment presentation should remain configuration-driven because issuer completeness, VAT handling, and archive/e-invoice readiness are still evolving
- `Depends on Communication Core`: user-facing communication preferences and message expectations must align with the current phase-1 email-first capability instead of assuming a finished multi-channel platform
- `Later-phase only`: translated CMS/page content operations, localized SEO metadata management, and additive languages beyond the current de/en baseline
- `Later-phase only`: full tenant-driven theming, advanced per-market payment/shipping matrices, complete multilingual content/template editing, and full compliance-driven presentation branching

## 6. Technical Foundations / Cross-Cutting

### Domain and application

- `Completed`: CRM no longer duplicates loyalty totals; `Customer.LoyaltyPointsTotal` and `LoyaltyPointEntry` are removed
- `Completed`: loyalty remains owned by `LoyaltyAccount` and `LoyaltyPointsTransaction`
- `Completed`: loyalty admin queues now include ops summaries and playbooks for accounts, scan sessions, and redemptions
- `Completed`: loyalty HTMX workspaces now keep localized success/error feedback visible inside fragment refresh flows
- `Completed`: Lead and Opportunity are part of the domain and application layers
- `Completed`: inventory supports warehouses, stock levels, transfers, suppliers, and purchase orders
- `Completed`: billing/accounting supports payments, financial accounts, journal entries, and expenses
- `Completed`: warehouse-aware fulfillment persists fulfillment context on order lines
- `Completed foundation`: payment domain lifecycle and provider audit trail now include Stripe webhook lifecycle processing, explicit provider-reference correlation, refund/reconciliation/dispute workbenches, and payment-editor provider audit trails backed by correlated `EventLog` entries for payment-intent, checkout-session, and transaction-reference history
- `Completed foundation`: phase-1 shipment/return admin queues now include configurable handoff-delay and tracking-grace thresholds from Site Settings, and shipping-method admin screens now expose operational subsets for missing rates, global coverage, and multi-rate review, so the current `WebAdmin` shipping-support surface is no longer the missing baseline
- `Planned / Near-term`: deepen shipment/return domain model and delivery exception lifecycle beyond the already-delivered `WebAdmin` operational queues
- `Completed foundation`: Communication Core now has a shared platform floor across domain/application/infrastructure rather than living only as feature-local helpers: email and channel dispatch audits are persisted as integration entities, shared notification abstractions and provider-backed sender implementations are registered centrally, template defaults are centralized, and invitation/activation/reset/phone-verification flows plus admin audit queries all run through the same cross-feature communication contract
- `Completed foundation`: expand Communication Core admin surfaces pragmatically; email test flow exists, and phase-1 SMS/WhatsApp test targets are now configurable for staged rollout visibility
- `Completed foundation`: merchant/tenant onboarding domain rules now have an explicit application/domain floor: businesses persist operational lifecycle state (`PendingApproval`, `Approved`, `Suspended`), activation-blocking access-state is machine-readable, onboarding customer-profile support is business-aware, and business create/update/lifecycle handlers keep tenant-scoped defaults, communication preferences, and approval/suspension transitions as first-class contract data instead of implicit UI-only behavior
- `Completed foundation`: settings domain architecture across global and business scopes is now explicit in domain/application code too: `SiteSetting` owns platform credentials/policies and shared defaults, `Business` owns tenant-scoped culture/time-zone/branding/admin-text/communication defaults, and the corresponding DTO/query/update/validation handlers preserve that split as a first-class contract instead of a purely WebAdmin-level convention

### WebApi

- `Completed`: mobile-used route surfaces have been reorganized with canonical audience-first routing while preserving compatibility aliases
- `Completed`: public/member loyalty, member commerce, profile, and storefront groundwork exists
- `Completed foundation`: mobile-used WebApi routes now have explicit source-level compatibility guards for bootstrap, profile phone verification, profile addresses/customer context, notifications device registration, and member-business onboarding aliases so backend refactors are less likely to silently break current mobile/member contracts
- `Planned / Near-term`: add admin/integration APIs only when WebAdmin and business/mobile scenarios demand them

### Mobile

- `Completed`: mobile apps remain operational and use shared canonical service abstractions
- `Completed`: `Darwin.Mobile.Business` is usable enough to influence delivery priorities
- `Completed`: `Darwin.Mobile.Business` invitation acceptance now works end-to-end against canonical business-auth endpoints
- `Completed foundation`: onboarding/account-lifecycle backend and admin support flows now satisfy current business-mobile usage through approval-aware auth, invitation acceptance, activation/reset/verification diagnostics, mobile operations triage, and business/member support handoffs
- `Completed`: `Darwin.Mobile.Business` now keeps `Home` and `Settings` available during `PendingApproval`, while `Scanner`, `Session`, `Dashboard`, and `Rewards` are approval-gated
- `Completed foundation`: mobile-used bootstrap and profile phone-verification route/alias compatibility now has explicit WebApi source guards, reducing the chance that backend refactors silently break current mobile contract paths

### Security and performance

- `Completed foundation`: WebApi pipeline order and auth endpoint throttling now have explicit source-level guard coverage, and WebAdmin admin lifecycle/destructive actions keep permission plus antiforgery protection under test-backed source guards
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin the business-override cache key and route/query/form `businessId` resolution chain inside `AdminTextLocalizer`, so localization overrides are less likely to drift silently behind broader infrastructure coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin normalize/filter/empty-fallback behavior inside `AdminTextOverrideCatalog`, so malformed or sparse admin text override payloads are less likely to drift silently behind broader localization coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin the default/normalize fallback map inside `SiteSettingCache`, so culture/JWT/WebAuthn/home-slug defaults are less likely to drift silently behind broader shared-helper coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin the anonymous/missing-claim/full-admin-bypass branches inside `PermissionRazorHelper`, so permission-gated Razor chrome is less likely to drift silently behind broader auth/helper coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin the constructor/null-request/absolute-build chain inside `CanonicalUrlService`, so canonical-path composition is less likely to drift silently behind broader shared-helper coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin suppress/page-clamp/HTMX-default behavior inside `PagerTagHelper`, so shared pagination rails are less likely to drift silently behind broader tag-helper coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin exact-match/controller-fallback/attribute-cleanup behavior inside `ActiveNavLinkTagHelper`, so shared active-navigation rails are less likely to drift silently behind broader tag-helper coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin reflection/split/timezone/current-value fallback behavior inside `SettingSelectTagHelper`, so settings-backed select rails are less likely to drift silently behind broader tag-helper coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin button-shell and conditional popover behavior inside `FieldHelpTagHelper`, so inline field-help rails are less likely to drift silently behind broader tag-helper coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin cookie-option and local-redirect behavior inside `CultureController`, so admin culture switching is less likely to drift silently behind broader startup/localization coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin cookie-auth/localization/shared-service registration inside `AddWebComposition`, so core admin composition is less likely to drift silently behind broader startup/composition coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin localization-provider ordering and middleware pipeline flow inside `UseWebStartupAsync`, so startup sequencing is less likely to drift silently behind broader startup/composition coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin Serilog/composition/startup handoff behavior inside `Program.cs`, so the root admin entrypoint is less likely to drift silently behind broader startup/composition coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin constructor-to-options registration behavior inside `ConfigureDisplayMetadataLocalization`, so display-metadata localization wiring is less likely to drift silently behind broader localization coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin constructor/null-display-attribute/display-name resolution behavior inside `SharedDisplayMetadataProvider`, so metadata-localization provider flow is less likely to drift silently behind broader localization coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin the method/documentation floor of `ISiteSettingCache` and `ICanonicalUrlService`, so shared settings/SEO service contracts are less likely to drift silently behind broader helper coverage
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin security/performance source guards now also pin the translation/language-option floor of `IAdminTextLocalizer`, so shared admin text contracts are less likely to drift silently behind broader localization coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin the method/documentation floor of `ICurrentUserService`, so current-user resolution is less likely to drift silently behind only WebAdmin-side implementation coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin the minimal attempt-throttle floor of `ILoginRateLimiter`, so login-rate-limit contracts are less likely to drift silently behind only infrastructure or WebApi-side coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin the method/documentation floor of `ISecurityStampService` and `ITotpService`, so auth-factor contracts are less likely to drift silently behind only infrastructure or consumer-side coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin the method/documentation floor of `IUserPasswordHasher` and `IWebAuthnService`, so password/WebAuthn auth contracts are less likely to drift silently behind only infrastructure or consumer-side coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin the method/documentation floor of `IEmailSender`, `ISmsSender`, and `IWhatsAppSender`, so notification contracts are less likely to drift silently behind only infrastructure or consumer-side coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin the method/documentation floor of `IInactiveReminderDispatcher`, `IBusinessInvitationLinkBuilder`, and `IWebAuthnSettingsProvider`, so reminder/onboarding/WebAuthn-settings contracts are less likely to drift silently behind only infrastructure or consumer-side coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin the method/documentation floor of `IAppDbContext` and `IClock`, so persistence/time contracts are less likely to drift silently behind only infrastructure or consumer-side coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin the access/refresh/revocation method floor of `IJwtTokenService`, so JWT token contracts are less likely to drift silently behind only infrastructure or consumer-side coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin the method/documentation floor of `IPermissionService`, `IHtmlSanitizer`, and `IAddOnPricingService`, so shared permission/HTML/catalog-pricing contracts are less likely to drift silently behind only implementation or consumer-side coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin the method/documentation floor of `IRelyingPartyFromSiteSettingsProvider` and `ISecretProtector`, so infrastructure WebAuthn/at-rest-secret contracts are less likely to drift silently behind only implementation coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin the method/documentation floor of `ILoyaltyPresentationService`, so WebApi loyalty reward-enrichment contracts are less likely to drift silently behind only implementation or consumer-side coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin the DB-fallback/split-trim/default chain inside `RelyingPartyFromSiteSettingsProvider`, so infrastructure WebAuthn relying-party hydration is less likely to drift silently behind only interface coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin registration/login ceremony wiring plus verification/error fallback behavior inside `Fido2WebAuthnService`, so infrastructure WebAuthn execution is less likely to drift silently behind only interface/provider coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin mutating-method gating, cache replay, in-progress conflict handling, and failure cleanup inside `IdempotencyMiddleware`, so WebApi retry-safety behavior is less likely to drift silently behind only broad pipeline coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin problem-details mapping, started-response guard, and write-failure handling inside `ErrorHandlingMiddleware`, so WebApi exception-envelope behavior is less likely to drift silently behind only broad pipeline coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin configuration validation and return/gateway URL shaping inside `StorefrontCheckoutUrlBuilder`, so storefront checkout handoff URLs are less likely to drift silently behind only consumer-side coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin the inactive-reminder worker loop, delay clamp, warning-threshold diagnostics, and default worker options, so background reminder orchestration is less likely to drift silently behind only broad hosting coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin cache-keying, selected-tier normalization, order-preserving enrichment, and missing-reward fallback behavior inside `LoyaltyPresentationService`, so WebApi loyalty UI shaping is less likely to drift silently behind only interface or consumer-side coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin the sliding-window allow/reset logic inside `MemoryLoginRateLimiter`, so in-memory login throttling is less likely to drift silently behind only interface-floor coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin random-stamp generation, constant-time compare, TOTP drift verification, and Base32 decode behavior inside `SecurityStampService` and `TotpService`, so auth-factor helper implementations are less likely to drift silently behind only interface-floor coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin Argon2 parameterization, password-byte wiping, and Data Protection secret-purpose wiring inside `Argon2PasswordHasher` and `DataProtectionSecretProtector`, so concrete password/secret protection primitives are less likely to drift silently behind only interface-floor coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin issuance, device-binding, refresh revocation, signing-key parsing, and active-business claim selection inside `JwtTokenService`, so concrete JWT token orchestration is less likely to drift silently behind only interface-floor coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin JwtBearer validation wiring, signing-parameter cache behavior, previous-key rollover, and negative-skew clamp inside `JwtBearerOptionsSetup` and `JwtSigningParametersProvider`, so WebApi JWT validation is less likely to drift silently behind only broad startup coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin hosted-service registration, handler auto-scan, JSON policy, startup branch ordering, and Program handoff inside the WebApi composition root, so WebApi bootstrapping is less likely to drift silently behind only broad startup/rate-limit coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin current-user claim resolution, dynamic permission-policy runtime wiring, and shared API problem-shaping inside WebApi auth/controller primitives, so JWT-authenticated API surfaces are less likely to drift silently behind only broad startup or interface-floor coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin login/refresh/logout orchestration, token-suffix logging, unauthorized logout-all fallback, and registration default-role/confirmation-email flow inside `AuthController`, so auth endpoint behavior is less likely to drift silently behind only route-level coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin invitation preview/accept DTO mapping and anonymous problem fallback behavior inside `BusinessAuthController`, so invitation-based business onboarding auth is less likely to drift silently behind only route-level coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin storefront checkout intent/order/payment/confirmation DTO mapping, hosted-checkout URL handoff, and invalid-order/outcome fallback behavior inside `PublicCheckoutController`, so high-traffic checkout orchestration is less likely to drift silently behind only route-level coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin anonymous-id fallback, cart mutation DTO mapping, reload-after-mutation behavior, and coupon/update/remove fallback handling inside `PublicCartController`, so high-traffic cart orchestration is less likely to drift silently behind only route-level coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin paging normalization, culture fallback, DTO projection, and product/page/menu not-found behavior inside `PublicCatalogController` and `PublicCmsController`, so high-traffic public content delivery is less likely to drift silently behind only broad anonymous-access coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin member order/invoice history paging, retry-payment gating, hosted-checkout handoff, document rendering, and deterministic action-path helpers inside `MemberOrdersController` and `MemberInvoicesController`, so member commerce detail flows are less likely to drift silently behind only authorize/route-level coverage
- `Completed foundation`: security/performance source guards now also pin profile self-service mapping, address-book mutation/reload behavior, linked-customer projections, and authenticated device-registration fallback logic inside `ProfileController`, `ProfileAddressesController`, and `NotificationsController`, so member self-service/runtime device flows are less likely to drift silently behind only authorize/alias coverage
- `Completed foundation`: identity password flows now enforce a shared localized password policy across registration, admin-set/change-password, and reset-password validators, and the highest-traffic WebAdmin password surfaces now expose the same bilingual policy hint instead of silently relying on a minimum-length-only rule
- `Completed foundation`: admin operational workspaces now have a source-guarded pagination/filter/search floor across businesses, business communications, billing, CRM, inventory, loyalty, media, mobile operations, orders, shipping, and identity, and the corresponding application query handlers keep queue-filter signatures wired so large operational datasets are no longer a soft-open admin concern
- `Completed foundation`: `Darwin.Worker` now processes pending and failed outgoing webhook deliveries in the background with event-log-backed JSON envelopes, HMAC-signed callback requests, poll/retry/max-attempt controls, and persisted response-code/status updates, so webhook dispatch no longer stays in a manual-only seeded/admin-observability state
- `Completed foundation`: inactive-reminder notification orchestration now also runs from `Darwin.Worker` with its own worker options and push-gateway configuration instead of staying attached to the `WebApi` request host, so reminder dispatch is no longer coupled to the API process lifecycle while the broader async/background rollout continues
- `Completed foundation`: async/background handling now covers reminder notifications, outgoing webhook delivery, and inbound Stripe/DHL payment/shipping callbacks through `Darwin.Worker`-hosted daemons plus a persisted provider-callback inbox, so provider-side callback application no longer depends on direct request-path mutation during the current phase
- `Completed foundation`: retry-safe integration and failure diagnostics across provider boundaries now include idempotency-middleware/source guards plus webhook-delivery retry-state classification, HTTP-response-aware failure diagnostics, escalation hints, and operator-facing callback triage across billing webhook workspaces

## 7. Localization Program

### Current state

- `Completed`: mobile apps already support bilingual operation
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin now runs on a `resx`-first localization architecture with shared UI resources, application validation resources, dedicated localization plumbing, centralized culture defaults, and platform/business override support
- `In Progress`: remaining communication content and broader non-admin localization still need continued coverage; low-traffic `WebAdmin` operator copy now has a source-guarded floor
- `Completed foundation`: shared business-discovery API conventions now route category, rating, and proximity validation through `ValidationResource`, and the business loyalty API now uses explicit localized fallback titles for reward-tier mutation validation failures, so another pocket of non-admin/public-business API chrome no longer depends on raw controller literals
- `Completed foundation`: lower-traffic admin CRM consent history and billing financial-account grids now localize consent/account type cells through the shared admin localizer instead of rendering raw type tokens
- `Completed foundation`: business mobile invitation preview now localizes operator-facing role and status labels while preserving canonical invitation values for acceptance logic and deep-link handoff
- `Completed foundation`: loyalty admin redemption/account-detail surfaces now localize scan outcome tokens through shared resources instead of rendering raw outcome strings like pending, accrued, redeemed, expired, or token-consumed
- `Completed foundation`: loyalty admin scan-session workspace now routes outcome tokens through the same shared localization path instead of leaving the queue-level outcome column on raw strings
- `Completed foundation`: CRM opportunity stages and invoice tax-profile badges now route through shared resource-backed localization in CRM and order-side invoice surfaces instead of rendering raw enum names
- `Completed foundation`: mobile-operations platform cells and CRM customer tax-profile summaries now route through shared resource-backed localization instead of rendering raw enum tokens in lower-traffic admin surfaces
- `Completed foundation`: business member, invitation, and staff-access role labels in low-traffic admin surfaces now route through shared resource-backed localization instead of rendering raw role enum tokens
- `Completed foundation`: mobile consumer rewards history now localizes loyalty transaction type chips through resource-backed display mapping instead of rendering raw `Accrual`, `Redemption`, or `Adjustment` tokens
- `Completed foundation`: mobile consumer customer-context now localizes CRM consent and interaction type/channel tokens instead of rendering raw `MarketingEmail`, `TermsOfService`, `Call`, `Meeting`, `Order`, `Support`, `Chat`, or `InPerson` values
- `Completed foundation`: business create/member/invitation forms in WebAdmin now localize business category and role select-option labels through shared resources instead of rendering raw enum names like `Cafe`, `Supermarket`, `Owner`, `Manager`, or `Staff`
- `Completed foundation`: the WebAdmin mobile-operations platform filter now localizes `Android` and `iOS` option labels through shared resources instead of rendering raw platform enum names in the operator queue chrome
- `Completed foundation`: loyalty account, scan-session, and redemption filter dropdowns in WebAdmin now localize enum-backed status and mode labels, and the reward-tier filter no longer leaves `Missing description` as a raw English literal
- `Completed foundation`: CRM customer, lead, opportunity, and segment queue filters in WebAdmin now localize lower-traffic operator labels instead of leaving raw English strings like `All customers`, `Closing soon`, or `Missing description` in controller-built dropdown chrome
- `Completed foundation`: orders queue filters in WebAdmin now localize lower-traffic dropdown labels for orders, payments, refunds, and invoices instead of leaving raw English strings like `All orders`, `All payments`, or `All refunds` in controller-built operator chrome
- `Completed foundation`: inventory queue filters in WebAdmin now localize lower-traffic dropdown labels for ledger, stock levels, purchase orders, and transfers instead of leaving raw English strings like `All ledger entries`, `All stock levels`, or `All transfers` in controller-built operator chrome
- `Completed foundation`: CRM segment playbooks in WebAdmin now route title, scope, and operator-action copy through shared resources instead of leaving two lower-traffic guidance cards on raw English sentences
- `Completed foundation`: inventory-ledger playbooks in WebAdmin now route title, scope, and operator-action copy through shared resources instead of leaving lower-traffic guidance cards on raw English sentences
- `Completed foundation`: inventory transfer and purchase-order playbooks in WebAdmin now route title, scope, and operator-action copy through shared resources instead of leaving lower-traffic guidance cards on raw English sentences

## 8. Decision Log

- `Decision made`: retire the legacy `/admin` and `/dashboard` redirects after `Darwin.WebAdmin` is functionally complete and post-completion testing confirms they are no longer needed
- `Completed foundation`: the legacy `/admin` and `/dashboard` compatibility redirects have now been removed after the completion audit/test pass, so `WebAdmin` no longer keeps a post-completion detour controller alive for deprecated entry paths
- `Decision made`: `MediaAsset` deletion follows a hybrid strategy: keep metadata-level soft delete now, then add reference-aware physical purge/orphan cleanup later
- `Decision made`: SME onboarding follows a staged rollout; phase 1 stays business-first, while deeper tenant/customer separation remains a later design/implementation decision
- `Decision made`: phase-1 business owner onboarding should support both assigning an existing platform user and invitation-first owner creation
- `Decision made`: the "last active owner cannot be removed or disabled" policy may be overridden only by `FullAdmin`, with required reason capture and explicit audit logging
- `Completed`: the `FullAdmin` override workflow for the "last active owner" policy now exists in business-member editing, with required reason entry, explicit UI warning, and persisted audit records
- `Future / Later phase`: add a site-setting option to require dual approval for the last-owner override path in enterprise-heavy deployments
- `Decision made`: invitation acceptance in phase 1 should support both token-entry and magic-link driven flows
- `Completed`: phase-1 invitation emails now include both the manual token path and a configurable magic-link path
- `Decision made`: business-scoped admins should receive delegated onboarding/support actions selectively; invitation issue/resend and reset-support are good candidates, while approval/suspension remain FullAdmin-only
- `Completed foundation`: WebAdmin now enforces that selective delegation model by allowing business-support operators into business list/member/invitation support flows while keeping business lifecycle, owner management, and archive actions FullAdmin-only
- `Completed foundation`: the legacy-encoded role-permissions workspace has been normalized into the current partial-driven editor path, and the `Roles/Permissions` view plus `_RolePermissionsEditorShell` are now source-guarded so future permission UX work does not regress back into encoding debt

- 2026-04-24: WebAdmin cleanup contracts are now source-guarded at the Razor view level. Unit tests enumerate all WebAdmin `.cshtml` files and fail if raw GET navigation/media attributes (`hx-get`, `href`, or `src`) regress to inline `@Url.Action(...)`, or if operator-facing timestamps regress to fixed `ToString("u")`; POST mutation and delete-modal `data-action` contracts remain intentionally outside this GET-navigation guard.

- 2026-04-24: WebAdmin HTMX mutation safety is now source-guarded too. Unit tests enumerate all WebAdmin `.cshtml` files and fail if any `hx-post` mutation surface is introduced without an `@Html.AntiForgeryToken()` in the posting Razor view, preserving the existing POST contracts while preventing tokenless HTMX mutations from landing later.

- 2026-04-24: WebAdmin delete-modal contracts are now source-guarded. The remaining shared delete `data-action="@Url.Action(...)"` buttons must keep the confirm modal target, id, rowVersion, HTMX target, and swap contract wired together; the user-address partial remains covered through its parent user editor shell, and the media queue now also sends `data-rowversion` with its delete action.

- 2026-04-24: WebAdmin HTMX target/swap consistency is now source-guarded. CRM lazy loaders and order detail tab loaders now declare explicit `hx-target="this"` beside their swap behavior, and unit tests enumerate every Razor tag with `hx-get`/`hx-post` to fail if target or swap behavior is left implicit.

- 2026-04-24: WebAdmin non-HTMX POST forms are now source-guarded alongside HTMX mutations. Unit tests enumerate every Razor `<form method="post">` and fail if the form body does not include an anti-forgery token, so login/account, culture/logout, full-page admin actions, and HTMX forms share one regression floor.

- 2026-04-24: WebAdmin controller-side POST anti-forgery is now source-guarded too. Unit tests enumerate controller `[HttpPost]` action attribute blocks and fail unless each action has `[ValidateAntiForgeryToken]` or an explicit `[IgnoreAntiforgeryToken]` exception, aligning the controller layer with the Razor form/token guards.

- 2026-04-24: WebAdmin admin-controller authorization is now source-guarded. Unit tests ensure `AdminBaseController` keeps `[PermissionAuthorize("AccessAdminPanel")]`, every controller under `Controllers/Admin` inherits from that protected base and avoids `[AllowAnonymous]`, and the non-admin controller surface remains explicitly limited to account and culture endpoints.

- 2026-04-24: WebAdmin raw error leakage is now source-guarded across the full controller surface, not only `Controllers/Admin`. Unit tests fail if any WebAdmin controller starts returning raw `ex.Message`, `result.Error`, or unsafe `Problem`/`BadRequest`/`TempData`/`ModelState` fallbacks instead of localized safe failure messages.

- 2026-04-24: WebAdmin anti-forgery ignore exceptions are now source-guarded. `UploadQuill` documents why Quill multipart uploads are the only `[IgnoreAntiforgeryToken]` exception, and unit tests fail if any other WebAdmin action introduces an anti-forgery bypass or if that exception loses its strict file-validation rationale.
